This architecture implements a strict separation between governance (baseline) and runtime state (overlay), enabling self-healing without polluting the source of truth.\n\n## Architecture Principles\n\n### 1. Immutability\n- **Baseline files are read-only at runtime**\n- Changes require explicit governance process\n- Filesystem permissions enforce immutability\n- No runtime modification allowed\n\n### 2. Separation of Concerns\n```\nbaseline/     ‚Üí Governance truth (immutable)\noverlay/      ‚Üí Runtime state (writable)\nactive/       ‚Üí Synthesized view (read-only)\n```\n\n### 3. Evidence-Based Validation\n- All operations produce evidence\n- Evidence stored in overlay/evidence/\n- Validation reports track compliance\n- Audit trail maintained\n\n## Directory Structure\n\n```\ncontrolplane/baseline/\n‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ config/                    # Core configuration files (10 files)\n‚îÇ   ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ root.config.yaml       # Main system configuration\n‚îÇ BASELINE_ARCHITECTURE.md # This file\n```\n\n## Component Descriptions\n\n### Configuration Files (config/)\n\n#### root.config.yaml\nMain system configuration defining core parameters, paths, and system-wide settings.\n\n#### root.devices.map\nDevice mapping rules that define how devices are accessed and managed within the root namespace.\n\n#### root.governance.yaml\nGovernance policies including approval workflows, change management, and compliance requirements.\n\n#### root.integrity.yaml\nIntegrity checking rules for verifying system component authenticity and detecting tampering.\n\n#### root.kernel.map\nKernel module mappings defining which kernel modules are allowed and how they\'re loaded.\n\n#### root.modules.yaml\nModule configuration specifying module parameters, dependencies, and loading order.\n\n#### root.naming-policy.yaml\nNaming conventions and policies for all system components, ensuring consistency.\n\n#### root.provenance.yaml\nProvenance tracking configuration for maintaining audit trails and change history.\n\n#### root.super-execution.yaml\nPrivileged execution rules defining when and how elevated privileges are granted.\n\n#### root.trust.yaml\nTrust model definitions including trust levels, verification methods, and trust boundaries.\n\n### Specifications (specifications/)\n\n#### root.specs.context.yaml\nContext specifications defining the operational environment and constraints.\n\n#### root.specs.logic.yaml\nLogic specifications defining behavioral rules and decision-making processes.\n\n#### root.specs.mapping.yaml\nMapping specifications defining relationships between components.\n\n#### root.specs.naming.yaml\nNaming specifications providing formal naming rules and patterns.\n\n#### root.specs.references.yaml\nReference specifications defining how components reference each other.\n\n### Registries (registries/)\n\n#### root.registry.modules.yaml\nCanonical registry of all modules with metadata, dependencies, and trust levels.\n\n#### root.registry.devices.yaml\nCanonical registry of all devices with types, permissions, and access rules.\n\n### Integration (integration/)\n\n#### root.integration.yaml\nCross-component integration rules ensuring components work together correctly.\n\n### Validation (validation/)\n\n#### gate-root-specs.yml\nValidation gate configuration defining validation checkpoints and requirements.\n\n#### validate-root-specs.py\nCore validation engine that executes validation rules and produces evidence.\n\n#### root.validation.vectors.yaml\nTest vectors for validating the validation system itself.\n\n## Data Flow\n\n### Bootstrap Sequence\n1. Load root.config.yaml (system configuration)\n2. Load specifications (formal rules)\n3. Load registries (component catalogs)\n4. Apply governance policies\n5. Enable integrity checking\n6. Validate complete system\n\n### Runtime Operation\n1. Check naming policy\n2. Verify trust level\n3. Validate against specifications\n4. Check registry\n5. Apply governance\n6. Record provenance\n7. Generate evidence\n\n### Validation Flow\n1. Load validation vectors\n2. Execute validation rules\n3. Check cross-component consistency\n4. Verify integration constraints\n5. Generate validation report\n6. Store evidence in overlay/\n\n## Integration Points\n\n### Config ‚Üî Specifications\n- Configurations must align with specifications\n- Naming policies must match naming specs\n- Trust policies must align with governance specs\n\n### Modules ‚Üî Devices\n- Modules can only access registered devices\n- Device permissions align with module trust levels\n- Module dependencies satisfied before device access\n\n### Governance ‚Üî Trust\n- Trust levels match governance classifications\n- Provenance tracking for all governed components\n- Integrity checks align with trust requirements\n\n### Naming ‚Üî Registry\n- All registered items follow naming policies\n- Module names match naming policy patterns\n- Registry entries use canonical names\n\n## Validation System\n\n### Validation Gates\n- **Pre-bootstrap**: Verify baseline integrity\n- **Post-bootstrap**: Verify system initialization\n- **Runtime**: Continuous validation\n- **Pre-shutdown**: Verify clean state\n\n### Validation Rules\n- **Structural**: File existence, format, syntax\n- **Semantic**: Logical consistency, completeness\n- **Integration**: Cross-component alignment\n- **Security**: Trust, integrity, provenance\n\n### Evidence Generation\nAll validation produces evidence stored in `overlay/evidence/`:\n- Validation reports (JSON)\n- Test results\n- Integrity checksums\n- Audit logs\n\n## Self-Healing Model\n\n### Scope\n- **Allowed**: Write to overlay/\n- **Allowed**: Extend registries via overlay\n- **Allowed**: Add runtime configurations\n- **Forbidden**: Modify baseline/\n- **Forbidden**: Modify active/\n\n### Process\n1. Detect issue via validation\n2. Determine if self-healable\n3. Generate overlay correction\n4. Validate correction\n5. Apply to overlay/\n6. Re-synthesize active/\n7. Generate evidence\n\n### Constraints\n- Must maintain integration constraints\n- Must pass all validation gates\n- Must preserve baseline immutability\n- Must generate complete evidence\n\n## Usage Guidelines\n\n### For System Administrators\n1. Never modify baseline/ directly\n2. Use overlay/ for runtime changes\n3. Review validation reports regularly\n4. Maintain evidence archives\n5. Follow governance processes for baseline updates\n\n### For Developers\n1. Reference baseline/ for canonical definitions\n2. Extend via overlay/ for customizations\n3. Use active/ for runtime queries\n4. Write validation tests for new components\n5. Document integration points\n\n### For Auditors\n1. Baseline/ is the governance truth\n2. Evidence/ contains validation proof\n3. Validation reports show compliance\n4. Provenance tracks all changes\n5. Integrity checks detect tampering\n\n## Maintenance\n\n### Baseline Updates\n1. Propose change via governance process\n2. Create change request with justification\n3. Review and approve via governance.yaml rules\n4. Update baseline/ files\n5. Run full validation suite\n6. Generate update evidence\n7. Commit to version control\n\n### Validation Updates\n1. Add new validation rules to validate-root-specs.py\n2. Add test vectors to root.validation.vectors.yaml\n3. Update gate-root-specs.yml if needed\n4. Test validation changes\n5. Document new validation requirements\n\n## Security Considerations\n\n### Immutability Enforcement\n- Filesystem permissions (read-only)\n- Version control (audit trail)\n- Integrity checking (tamper detection)\n- Validation gates (compliance verification)\n\n### Trust Boundaries\n- Baseline ‚Üí Overlay (one-way reference)\n- Overlay ‚Üí Active (synthesis only)\n- Active ‚Üí Runtime (read-only view)\n\n### Audit Trail\n- All changes tracked in provenance\n- Evidence generated for all operations\n- Validation reports archived\n- Governance approvals recorded\n\n## Troubleshooting\n\n### Validation Failures\n1. Check validation report in overlay/evidence/\n2. Review specific failed rules\n3. Verify baseline file integrity\n4. Check cross-component consistency\n5. Review recent overlay changes\n\n### Integration Issues\n1. Check root.integration.yaml rules\n2. Verify component references\n3. Check registry completeness\n4. Validate naming consistency\n5. Now let me create the final documentation and prepare for Git commit:\n\n<function_calls>\n<create-file file_path="controlplane/CONTROLPLANE_USAGE.md">\n# Controlplane Usage Guide\n\n## Overview\n\nThe Controlplane architecture implements a **Baseline + Overlay + Active** design pattern that separates immutable governance truth from runtime state, enabling self-healing without polluting the source of truth.\n\n## Architecture Components\n\n### 1. Baseline (Immutable Governance Truth)\n**Location**: `controlplane/baseline/`  \n**Access**: Read-only  \n**Purpose**: Contains the canonical, immutable governance configuration\n\n**Structure**:\n```\nbaseline/\n‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ config/              # Core configuration files (10 files)\n‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ specifications/      # Formal specifications (5 files)\n‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ registries/          # Component registries (2 files)\n‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ integration/         # Integration rules (1 file)\n‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ validation/          # Validation system (3 files)\n‚îî‚îÄ‚îÄ documentation/       # Architecture documentation\n```\n\n**Key Principle**: Baseline files are **never modified at runtime**. All changes require explicit governance approval and version control.\n\n### 2. Overlay (Writable Runtime State)\n**Location**: `controlplane/overlay/`  \n**Access**: Read-write  \n**Purpose**: Stores runtime state, self-healing corrections, and operational evidence\n\n**Structure**:\n```\noverlay/\n‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ config/              # Runtime configuration extensions\n‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ evidence/            # Validation evidence and reports\n‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ runtime/             # Runtime state data\n‚îî‚îÄ‚îÄ logs/                # Operational logs\n```\n\n**Key Principle**: Self-healing operations **only write to overlay**. This preserves baseline integrity while allowing system adaptation.\n\n### 3. Active (Synthesized View)\n**Location**: `controlplane/active/`  \n**Access**: Read-only  \n**Purpose**: Provides a unified, read-only view of baseline + overlay\n\n**Key Principle**: Active view is **synthesized on-demand** and never directly modified.\n\n## Quick Start\n\n### Running Validation\n\nExecute the validation system to verify baseline integrity:\n\n```bash\n# Run validation\npython3 controlplane/baseline/validation/validate-root-specs.py\n\n# Check validation results\ncat controlplane/overlay/evidence/validation/validation.report.json\n\n# View human-readable report\ncat controlplane/overlay/evidence/validation/validation.report.md\n```\n\n### Accessing Configuration\n\n```bash\n# Source environment variables\nsource root.env.sh\n\n# Access baseline configuration\ncat $MACHINENATIVEOPS_BASELINE_CONFIG/root.config.yaml\n\n# Access overlay evidence\nls -la $MACHINENATIVEOPS_OVERLAY_EVIDENCE/\n\n# View validation manifest\ncat $MACHINENATIVEOPS_OVERLAY_EVIDENCE/validation/controlplane.manifest.json\n```\n\n### Environment Variables\n\nThe following environment variables are available after sourcing `root.env.sh`:\n\n**Controlplane Paths**:\n- `MACHINENATIVEOPS_CONTROLPLANE`: Root controlplane directory\n- `MACHINENATIVEOPS_BASELINE`: Baseline directory\n- `MACHINENATIVEOPS_OVERLAY`: Overlay directory\n- `MACHINENATIVEOPS_ACTIVE`: Active view directory\n\n**Baseline Subdirectories**:\n- `MACHINENATIVEOPS_BASELINE_CONFIG`: Baseline configuration\n- `MACHINENATIVEOPS_BASELINE_SPECS`: Baseline specifications\n- `MACHINENATIVEOPS_BASELINE_REGISTRIES`: Baseline registries\n- `MACHINENATIVEOPS_BASELINE_INTEGRATION`: Integration rules\n- `MACHINENATIVEOPS_BASELINE_VALIDATION`: Validation system\n- `MACHINENATIVEOPS_BASELINE_DOCS`: Documentation\n\n**Overlay Subdirectories**:\n- `MACHINENATIVEOPS_OVERLAY_CONFIG`: Runtime configuration\n- `MACHINENATIVEOPS_OVERLAY_EVIDENCE`: Validation evidence\n- `MACHINENATIVEOPS_OVERLAY_RUNTIME`: Runtime state\n- `MACHINENATIVEOPS_OVERLAY_LOGS`: Operational logs\n\n**Validation Tools**:\n- `MACHINENATIVEOPS_VALIDATOR`: Validation script path\n- `MACHINENATIVEOPS_VALIDATION_GATE`: Validation gate config\n- `MACHINENATIVEOPS_VALIDATION_VECTORS`: Test vectors\n\n## Common Operations\n\n### 1. Viewing Baseline Configuration\n\n```bash\n# List all baseline config files\nls -la controlplane/baseline/config/\n\n# View specific configuration\ncat controlplane/baseline/config/root.config.yaml\ncat controlplane/baseline/config/root.governance.yaml\ncat controlplane/baseline/config/root.trust.yaml\n```\n\n### 2. Checking Validation Status\n\n```bash\n# View latest validation report\ncat controlplane/overlay/evidence/validation/validation.report.json | jq \'.pass\'\n\n# View validation summary\ncat controlplane/overlay/evidence/validation/validation.report.json | jq \'.summary\'\n\n# Check specific stage results\ncat controlplane/overlay/evidence/validation/validation.report.json | jq \'.stages.structural\'\n```\n\n### 3. Reviewing Evidence\n\n```bash\n# List all evidence\nfind controlplane/overlay/evidence -type f\n\n# View validation manifest\ncat controlplane/overlay/evidence/validation/controlplane.manifest.json\n\n# Read markdown report\nless controlplane/overlay/evidence/validation/validation.report.md\n```\n\n### 4. Extending Configuration (Self-Healing)\n\nWhen the system needs to adapt, it writes to overlay:\n\n```bash\n# Create overlay configuration extension\ncat > controlplane/overlay/config/custom-extension.yaml << EOF\nmetadata:\n  name: custom-extension\n  type: overlay\n  extends: baseline/config/root.config.yaml\n\nconfiguration:\n  custom_setting: value\nEOF\n\n# Validate the extension\npython3 controlplane/baseline/validation/validate-root-specs.py\n```\n\n## Validation System\n\n### Validation Stages\n\nThe validation system executes five stages:\n\n1. **Structural Validation**: Verifies directory structure and file existence\n2. **Syntax Validation**: Checks YAML syntax and structure\n3. **Semantic Validation**: Validates logical consistency\n4. **Integration Validation**: Verifies cross-component integration\n5. **Security Validation**: Checks security properties\n\n### Validation Reports\n\nAfter validation, three artifacts are generated:\n\n1. **validation.report.json**: Machine-readable validation results\n2. **validation.report.md**: Human-readable markdown report\n3. **controlplane.manifest.json**: Validation manifest with metadata\n\n### Success Criteria\n\nValidation passes when:\n- All 50 checks pass across all stages\n- No critical failures detected\n- Evidence successfully generated\n- Report shows `"pass": true`\n\n## Integration with Bootstrap\n\nThe controlplane is integrated with the root bootstrap process:\n\n### root.bootstrap.yaml\n\n```yaml\nspec:\n  controlplane:\n    enabled: true\n    baseline_path: controlplane/baseline\n    overlay_path: controlplane/overlay\n    active_path: controlplane/active\n    validation:\n      enabled: true\n      validator: controlplane/baseline/validation/validate-root-specs.py\n      on_failure: halt_system\n```\n\n### root.fs.map\n\nFilesystem mappings include:\n- `controlplane_baseline`: Read-only baseline directory\n- `controlplane_overlay`: Read-write overlay directory\n- `controlplane_active`: Read-only active view\n\n### root.env.sh\n\nEnvironment variables provide easy access to all controlplane paths and tools.\n\n## Best Practices\n\n### DO ‚úÖ\n\n1. **Always validate after changes**: Run validation after any configuration changes\n2. **Use overlay for runtime state**: Write all runtime data to overlay\n3. **Review evidence regularly**: Check validation reports and evidence\n4. **Follow naming conventions**: Use consistent naming from baseline policies\n5. **Document extensions**: Document any overlay extensions clearly\n6. **Version control baseline**: Keep baseline under strict version control\n7. **Archive evidence**: Maintain evidence archives for audit trails\n\n### DON\'T ‚ùå\n\n1. **Never modify baseline at runtime**: Baseline is immutable\n2. **Don\'t write to active**: Active view is read-only\n3. **Don\'t bypass validation**: Always run validation gates\n4. **Don\'t ignore validation failures**: Address failures immediately\n5. **Don\'t pollute baseline**: Keep runtime state in overlay\n6. **Don\'t skip evidence generation**: Always generate evidence\n7. **Don\'t modify validation system**: Validation is part of baseline\n\n## Troubleshooting\n\n### Validation Failures\n\nIf validation fails:\n\n1. Check the validation report:\n   ```bash\n   cat controlplane/overlay/evidence/validation/validation.report.json | jq \'.stages[] | select(.passed == false)\'\n   ```\n\n2. Review specific failed checks:\n   ```bash\n   cat controlplane/overlay/evidence/validation/validation.report.md\n   ```\n\n3. Fix the issues and re-run validation:\n   ```bash\n   python3 controlplane/baseline/validation/validate-root-specs.py\n   ```\n\n### Missing Files\n\nIf files are missing:\n\n1. Recreate missing files from templates\n\n### Permission Issues\n\nIf permission errors occur:\n\n1. Verify baseline is read-only (in production)\n2. Verify overlay is writable\n3. Check filesystem permissions in root.fs.map\n\n## Advanced Topics\n\n### Custom Validation Rules\n\nTo add custom validation rules:\n\n1. Edit `controlplane/baseline/validation/validate-root-specs.py`\n2. Add new validation methods\n3. Update validation stages\n4. Add test vectors to `root.validation.vectors.yaml`\n5. Test thoroughly before deployment\n\n### Overlay Extensions\n\nTo create overlay extensions:\n\n1. Create extension file in `controlplane/overlay/config/`\n2. Reference baseline configuration\n3. Add only delta/extension data\n4. Run validation to verify\n5. Document the extension purpose\n\n### Evidence Management\n\nEvidence is automatically generated and stored in:\n- `controlplane/overlay/evidence/validation/`\n\nManage evidence:\n```bash\n# Archive old evidence\ntar -czf evidence-$(date +%Y%m%d).tar.gz controlplane/overlay/evidence/\n\n# Clean old evidence (keep last 90 days)\nfind controlplane/overlay/evidence -type f -mtime +90 -delete\n```\n\n## Security Considerations\n\n### Immutability Enforcement\n\nIn production:\n- Baseline directory should be mounted read-only\n- Filesystem permissions enforce immutability\n- Version control tracks all baseline changes\n\n### Trust Boundaries\n\n- **Baseline ‚Üí Overlay**: One-way reference only\n- **Overlay ‚Üí Active**: Synthesis only, no direct modification\n- **Active ‚Üí Runtime**: Read-only view\n\n### Audit Trail\n\nAll operations generate evidence:\n- Validation reports\n- Integrity checksums\n- Provenance tracking\n- Change logs\n\n## Support and Resources\n\n### Documentation\n\n- **Architecture**: `controlplane/baseline/documentation/BASELINE_ARCHITECTURE.md`\n- **Usage Guide**: This file\n- **Validation Gate**: `controlplane/baseline/validation/gate-root-specs.yml`\n\n### Tools\n\n- **Validator**: `controlplane/baseline/validation/validate-root-specs.py`\n- **Bootstrap**: `root.bootstrap.yaml`\n- **Environment**: `root.env.sh`\n- **Filesystem Map**: `root.fs.map`\n\n### Getting Help\n\nFor issues or questions:\n1.
